 "cells": [
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "# ニューラルネットワーク\n",
    "\n",
    "## 12.1 人工ニューラルネットワークによる複雑な関数のモデリング\n",
    "\n",
    "- 多層フィードフォワードニューラルネットワーク (multi-layer feedforward neural netwrok, Multi-Layer perceptron: MLP)\n",
    "\n",
    "  - *入力層*, *隠れ層* (hidden layer), *出力層* から成る\n",
    "  \n",
    "- 活性化ユニット $a_i^{(l)}$\n",
    "  \n",
    "  - $l$ 番目の層の $i$ 番目の活性化ユニット\n",
    "  - $${\\boldsymbol a^{(l)}} = \\left[\\begin{array}{c} a_0^{(1)}\\\\ a_1^{(1)}\\\\ \\vdots \\\\ a_m^{(1)}\\\\ \\end{array}\\right]$$\n",
    "  - $l$ 番目の各ユニットは、重み係数に基づき $l + 1$ 層のすべてのユニットと結合する\n",
    "  \n",
    "- 重み（結合） $w_{j,k}^{(l)}$\n",
    "\n",
    "  - $l$ 層 $k$ 番目のユニットと $l + 1$ 層 $j$ 番目のユニットとの結合\n",
    "  - $l$ 層と $l + 1$ 層の結合の重みの行列表現 ${\\boldsymbol W}^{(l)} = \\left[\\begin{array}{c c c c c}\n",
    "  w_{0,1}^{(l)} & w_{0,1}^{(l)} & \\ldots & & w_{m,1}^{(l)}\\\\ \n",
    "  & \\ddots & & & \\\\\n",
    "  \\vdots & & w_{j,k}^{(l)} & & \\\\\n",
    "  &  & & \\ddots & \\\\\n",
    "  w_{0,h}^{(l)} & w_{0,h}^{(l)} & \\ldots & & w_{m,h}^{(l)}\\\\ \n",
    "  \\end{array}\\right]\\in \\mathbb{R}^{h \\times \\left(m + 1\\right)}$\n",
    "    \n",
    "    - $h$: $l + 1$ 層のユニット数\n",
    "    - $m + 1$: $l$ 層のユニット（除くバイアスユニット）数 ($m$) + バイアスユニット数 ($1$)\n",
    "  \n",
    "- ニューラルネットワークは、 *一対全* (One-vs-All) の一般化手法を用いて多クラス分類を実行できる\n",
    "- フォワードプロパゲーション（順伝播法, forward propagation）\n",
    "\n",
    "  - 活性化ユニット $a_1^{(2)}$ の計算\n",
    "  \n",
    "    - 総入力: $z_1^{(2)} = a_0^{(1)}w_{1,0}^{(1)} + a_1^{(1)}w_{1,1}^{(1)} + \\dots + a_0^{(m)}w_{1,m}^{(1)}$\n",
    "    - 活性化関数（シグモイド関数）: $\\phi\\left(z\\right) = \\frac{1}{1+e^{-z}}$\n",
    "    - $a_1^{(2)} = \\phi\\left(z_1^{(2)}\\right)$\n",
    "    - 簡潔に記述すると以下の式に要約される\n",
    "    \n",
    "      - ${\\boldsymbol z^{(2)}} = {\\boldsymbol W}^{(1)}{\\boldsymbol a}^{(1)}$\n",
    "      - ${\\boldsymbol a^{(2)}} = \\phi\\left({\\boldsymbol z^{(2)}}\\right)$\n",
    "\n",
    "- MLP の学習ステップ（以下のステップを繰り返す）\n",
    "\n",
    "  1. 入力層にトレーニングデータを入力し、出力層へ順方向で伝播させる\n",
    "  2. コスト関数を用いて、出力の誤差を計算する\n",
    "  3. 誤差を逆方向に伝播させ、モデルを更新する"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "## 12.2 手書きの数字を分類する"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "### 12.2.1 MNIST データセットを取得する\n",
    "\n",
    "- MNIST (Mixed National Institute of Standards and Technology)\n",
    "- 手書きの数字\n",
    "- ベンチマーク用に使う"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 56,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": true
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "import os\n",
    "import struct\n",
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def load_mnist(path, kind='train'):\n",
    "    \"\"\" MNIST データのロード \"\"\"\n",
    "    labels_path = os.path.join(path, '{}-labels-idx1-ubyte'.format(kind))\n",
    "    images_path = os.path.join(path, '{}-images-idx3-ubyte'.format(kind))\n",
    "\n",
    "    with open(labels_path, 'rb') as lbpath:\n",
    "        # :magic: マジックナンバー\n",
    "        # :n: アイテムの個数\n",
    "        # :'>II': ビッグエンディアン, 符号なし整数 (4 byte), 符号なし整数 (4 byte)\n",
    "        magic, n = struct.unpack('>II', lbpath.read(8))\n",
    "        # ラベル\n",
    "        labels = np.fromfile(lbpath, dtype=np.uint8)\n",
    "\n",
    "    with open(images_path, 'rb') as imgpath:\n",
    "        # :magic: マジックナンバー\n",
    "        # :num: アイテムの個数\n",
    "        # :rows: 行数\n",
    "        # :cols: 列数\n",
    "        magic, num, rows, cols = struct.unpack(\">IIII\", imgpath.read(16))\n",
    "        images = np.fromfile(imgpath, dtype=np.uint8).reshape(len(labels), 784)\n",
    "\n",
    "    return images, labels"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 112,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": false
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [

    "### 12.2.2 多層パーセプトロンを実装する\n",
    "\n",
    "- MNIST のデータを分類する MLP を実装する\n",
    "- 入力層・隠れ層・出力層の 3 層で構成する\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 120,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": false
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "from scipy.special import expit\n",
    "import sys\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "class NeuralNetMLP(object):\n",
    "\n",
    "    def __init__(\n",
    "        self,\n",
    "        n_output,\n",
    "        n_features,\n",
    "        n_hidden=30,\n",
    "        l1=0.0,\n",
    "        l2=0.0,\n",
    "        epochs=500,\n",
    "        eta=0.001,\n",
    "        alpha=0.0,\n",
    "        decrease_const=0.0,\n",
    "        shuffle=True,\n",
    "        minibatches=1,\n",
    "        random_state=None,\n",
    "    ):\n",
    "        \"\"\" NeuralNetMLP の初期化\n",
    "\n",
    "        :param int n_output: 出力ユニット数\n",
    "        :param int n_features: 入力ユニット数\n",
    "        :param int n_hidden: 隠れユニット数\n",
    "        :param float l1: L1 正則化のλパラメータ\n",
    "        :param float l2: L2 正則化のλパラメータ\n",
    "        :param int epochs: エポック数\n",
    "        :param float eta: 学習率の初期値\n",
    "        :param float alpha: モーメンタム学習の 1 つ前の勾配の係数\n",
    "        :param float decrease_const: 適応学習率の減少定数 d\n",
    "        :param bool shuffle: データのシャッフル\n",
    "        :param int minibatches: 各エポックでのミニバッチ数\n",
    "        \"\"\"\n",
    "        np.random.seed(random_state)\n",
    "        self.n_output = n_output\n",
    "        self.n_features = n_features\n",
    "        self.n_hidden = n_hidden\n",
    "        self.w1, self.w2 = self._initialize_weights() # 重みの初期化\n",
    "        self.l1 = l1\n",
    "        self.l2 = l2\n",
    "        self.epochs = epochs\n",
    "        self.eta = eta\n",
    "        self.alpha = alpha\n",
    "        self.decrease_const = decrease_const\n",
    "        self.shuffle = shuffle\n",
    "        self.minibatches = minibatches\n",
    "\n",
    "    def _encode_labels(self, y, k):\n",
    "        \"\"\" ラベルのエンコード\n",
    "\n",
    "        :rtype: numpy.ndarray\n",
    "        \"\"\"\n",
    "        onehot = np.zeros((k, y.shape[0]))\n",
    "        for idx, val in enumerate(y):\n",
    "            onehot[val, idx] = 1.0\n",
    "        return onehot\n",
    "\n",
    "    def _initialize_weights(self):\n",
    "        \"\"\" 重みの初期化\n",
    "\n",
    "        :rtype: Tuple[numpy.ndarray, numpy.ndarray]\n",
    "        \"\"\"\n",
    "        w1 = np.random.uniform(-1.0, 1.0,\n",
    "                               size=self.n_hidden * (self.n_features + 1))\n",
    "        w1 = w1.reshape(self.n_hidden, self.n_features + 1)\n",
    "        w2 = np.random.uniform(-1.0, 1.0,\n",
    "                               size=self.n_output * (self.n_hidden + 1))\n",
    "        w2 = w2.reshape(self.n_output, self.n_hidden + 1)\n",
    "        return w1, w2\n",
    "\n",
    "    def _sigmoid(self, z):\n",
    "        \"\"\" シグモイド関数\n",
    "\n",
    "        :rtype: float\n",
    "        \"\"\"\n",
    "        return expit(z)\n",
    "\n",
    "    def _sigmoid_gradient(self, z):\n",
    "        \"\"\" シグモイド関数の勾配（偏微分係数）\n",
    "\n",
    "        :rtype: float\n",
    "        \"\"\"\n",
    "        return (lambda sg: sg * (1 - sg))(self._sigmoid(z))\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "    def _add_bias_unit(self, X, how='column'):\n",
    "        \"\"\" バイアスユニットの追加\n",
    "\n",
    "        :param numpy.ndarray X: X\n",
    "        :param str how: ``column`` or ``row``\n",
    "        :rtype: numpy.ndarray\n",
    "        \"\"\"\n",
    "        if how == 'column':\n",
    "            X_new = np.ones((X.shape[0], X.shape[1] + 1))\n",
    "            X_new[:, 1:] = X\n",
    "        elif how == 'row':\n",
    "            X_new = np.ones((X.shape[0] + 1, X.shape[1]))\n",
    "            X_new[1:, :] = X\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            raise ValueError('``how`` must be ``column`` or ``row``')\n",
    "        return X_new\n",
    "            \n",
    "\n",
    "    def _feedforward(self, X, w1, w2):\n",
    "        \"\"\" フィードフォワード \"\"\"\n",
    "        a1 = self._add_bias_unit(X, how='column')\n",
    "        z2 = w1.dot(a1.T)  # 隠れ層の総入力\n",
    "        a2 = self._sigmoid(z2)  # 隠れ層の活性化関数\n",
    "        a2 = self._add_bias_unit(a2, how='row')  # a2 + バイアスユニット\n",
    "        z3 = w2.dot(a2)  # 出力層の総入力\n",
    "        a3 = self._sigmoid(z3)  # 出力層の活性化関数\n",
    "        return a1, z2, a2, z3, a3\n",
    "\n",
    "    def _L2_reg(self, lambda_, w1, w2):\n",
    "        \"\"\" L2 ペナルティ項の係数 \"\"\"\n",
    "        return (lambda_ / 2.0) * (np.sum(w1[:, 1:] ** 2) +\n",
    "                np.sum(w2[:, 1:] ** 2))\n",
    "\n",
    "    def _L1_reg(self, lambda_, w1, w2):\n",
    "        \"\"\" L1 ペナルティ項の係数 \"\"\"\n",
    "        return (lambda_ / 2.0) * (np.abs(w1[:, 1:]).sum() +\n",
    "                np.abs(w2[:, 1:]).sum())\n",
    "\n",
    "    def _get_cost(self, y_enc, output, w1, w2):\n",
    "        \"\"\" コストの計算 \"\"\"\n",
    "        term1 = - y_enc * (np.log(output))\n",
    "        term2 = (1.0 - y_enc) * np.log(1.0 - output)\n",
    "        cost = np.sum(term1 - term2)\n",
    "        L1_term = self._L1_reg(self.l1, w1, w2)\n",
    "        L2_term = self._L2_reg(self.l2, w1, w2)\n",
    "        cost = cost + L1_term + L2_term\n",
    "        return cost\n",
    "\n",
    "    def _get_gradient(self, a1, a2, a3, z2, y_enc, w1, w2):\n",
    "        \"\"\" 勾配の計算\n",
    "        \n",
    "        :param y_enc: 教師信号\n",
    "        \"\"\"\n",
    "        # バックプロパゲーション\n",
    "        delta3 = a3 - y_enc  # 出力層の誤差ベクトル\n",
    "        z2 = self._add_bias_unit(z2, how='row')  \n",
    "        delta2 = w2.T.dot(delta3) * self._sigmoid_gradient(z2) # 隠れ層の誤差項\n",
    "        delta2 = delta2[1:, :]\n",
    "        grad1 = delta2.dot(a1)  # コスト関数の偏微分係数の計算\n",
    "        grad2 = delta3.dot(a2.T)  # コスト関数の偏微分係数の計算\n",
    "\n",
    "        # 正則化 (勾配 + 正則化項 λ)\n",
    "        grad1[:, 1:] += self.l2 * w1[:, 1:]\n",
    "        grad1[:, 1:] += self.l1 * np.sign(w1[:, 1:])\n",
    "        grad2[:, 1:] += self.l2 * w2[:, 1:]\n",
    "        grad2[:, 1:] += self.l1 * np.sign(w2[:, 1:])\n",
    "        return grad1, grad2\n",
    "\n",
    "    def predict(self, X):\n",
    "        \"\"\" フィードフォワードによる予測 \"\"\"\n",
    "        a1, z2, a2, z3, a3 = self._feedforward(X, self.w1, self.w2)\n",
    "        y_pred = np.argmax(z3, axis=0)\n",
    "        return y_pred\n",
    "\n",
    "    def fit(self, X, y, print_progress=False):\n",
    "        self.cost_ = []\n",
    "        X_data, y_data = X.copy(), y.copy()\n",
    "        y_enc = self._encode_labels(y, self.n_output)\n",
    "        delta_w1_prev = np.zeros(self.w1.shape)\n",
    "        delta_w2_prev = np.zeros(self.w2.shape)\n",
    "        for i in range(self.epochs):\n",
    "\n",
    "            # adaptive learning rate\n",
    "            self.eta /= (1 + self.decrease_const * i)\n",
    "            if print_progress:\n",
    "                sys.stderr.write('\\rEpoch: %d/%d' % (i + 1, self.epochs))\n",
    "                sys.stderr.flush()\n",
    "            if self.shuffle:\n",
    "                idx = np.random.permutation(y_data.shape[0])\n",
    "                X_data, y_enc = X_data[idx], y_enc[:, idx]\n",
    "            mini = np.array_split(range(y_data.shape[0]), self.minibatches)\n",
    "            for idx in mini:\n",
    "\n",
    "                # フィードフォワード\n",
    "                a1, z2, a2, z3, a3 = self._feedforward(\n",
    "                    X_data[idx],\n",
    "                    self.w1,\n",
    "                    self.w2,\n",
    "                )\n",
    "                cost = self._get_cost(\n",
    "                        y_enc=y_enc[:, idx],\n",
    "                        output=a3,\n",
    "                        w1=self.w1,\n",
    "                        w2=self.w2\n",
    "                )\n",
    "                self.cost_.append(cost)\n",
    "                # バックプロパゲーションによる勾配の計算\n",
    "                grad1, grad2 = self._get_gradient(a1=a1, a2=a2, a3=a3, z2=z2,\n",
    "                                                  y_enc=y_enc[:, idx],\n",
    "                                                  w1=self.w1,\n",
    "                                                  w2=self.w2)\n",
    "                # 重みの更新\n",
    "                delta_w1, delta_w2 = self.eta * grad1, self.eta * grad2\n",
    "                self.w1 -= (delta_w1 + (self.alpha * delta_w1_prev))  # 勾配を下る（勾配 + モーメンタム項）\n",
    "                self.w2 -= (delta_w2 + (self.alpha * delta_w2_prev))  # 勾配を下る（勾配 + モーメンタム項）\n",
    "                delta_w1_prev, delta_w2_prev = delta_w1, delta_w2\n",
    "                \n",
    "        return self"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",

    "    decrease_const=0.00001,\n",

   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "## 12.3 人工ニューラルネットワークをトレーニングする\n",
    "\n",
    "### 12.3.1 ロジスティック関数を計算する\n",
    "\n",
    "出力層における活性化関数 $\\phi\\left(z\\right)$ の負の対数尤度である、コストを最小化することが目的（たぶん）である。\n",
    "\n",
    "出力層 $l$ のコスト $J\\left({\\boldsymbol w}\\right)$ は次の通り算出される\n",
    "\n",
    "$$J\\left({\\boldsymbol w}\\right) = - \\left[ \\sum_{i=1}^n y_i\\log\\left(a_i^{(l)}\\right) + \\left(1 - y_i\\right)\\log\\left(1 - a_i^{(l)}\\right)  \\right]$$\n",
    "\n",
    "L1/L2 正則化項は次のように定義される\n",
    "\n",
    "$$L1 = \\frac{\\lambda}{2}\\left|\\left|{\\boldsymbol w}\\right|\\right|^1_1 = \\frac{\\lambda}{2}\\sum^m_j\\left|w_j\\right|$$\n",
    "$$L2 = \\frac{\\lambda}{2}\\left|\\left|{\\boldsymbol w}\\right|\\right|^2_2 = \\frac{\\lambda}{2}\\sum^m_jw^2_j$$\n",
    "\n",
    "したがって、たとえば、 L2 正則化項をコスト関数に追加すると次のようになる\n",
    "\n",
    "$$J\\left({\\boldsymbol w}\\right) = - \\left[ \\sum_{i=1}^n y_i\\log\\left(a_i^{(l)}\\right) + \\left(1 - y_i\\right)\\log\\left(1 - a_i^{(l)}\\right)  \\right] + \\frac{\\lambda}{2}\\left|\\left|{\\boldsymbol w}\\right|\\right|^2_2$$\n",
    "\n",
    "また、出力層 $l$ におけるコスト $J\\left({\\boldsymbol w}\\right)$ をすべての教師信号 $p$ について足し上げると以下のようになる\n",
    "\n",
    "$$J(w) = - \\left[ \\sum_{p=1}\\sum_{i=1}^n y_{ip}\\log\\left(a_{ip}^{(l)}\\right) + \\left(1 - y_{ip}\\right)\\log\\left(1 - a_{ip}^{(l)}\\right)  \\right]$$\n",
    "\n",
    "さらに、 L2 正則化項として、すべての重みの二乗和を足す"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": true
   },
   "source": [
    "### 12.3.2 バックプロパゲーションを使ってニューラルネットワークをトレーニングする\n",
    "\n",
    "隠れ層の総入力\n",
    "\n",
    "$${\\boldsymbol Z}^{(2)} = {\\boldsymbol W}^{(1)}\\left[{\\boldsymbol A}^{(1)}\\right]^T$$\n",
    "\n",
    "隠れ層の出力\n",
    "\n",
    "$${\\boldsymbol A}^{(2)} = \\phi\\left({\\boldsymbol Z}^{(2)}\\right)$$\n",
    "\n",
    "出力層の総入力\n",
    "\n",
    "$${\\boldsymbol Z}^{(3)} = {\\boldsymbol W}^{(3)}{\\boldsymbol A}^{(2)}$$\n",
    "\n",
    "出力層の出力\n",
    "\n",
    "$${\\boldsymbol A}^{(3)} = \\phi\\left({\\boldsymbol Z}^{(3)}\\right)$$"
   ]
  },
